 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The address for each executive officer is c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West
Street, New York, New York 10282. Each officer holds office at the pleasure of the Board until the next election of officers or until his or her successor is duly elected and qualifies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Justin Betzen.</B> Mr. Betzen is a managing director and senior underwriter in Private Credit within Goldman Sachs Asset Management,
focused on middle market lending in the Americas. He is a member of the BDC Investment Committee and the Private Credit Investment Subcommittee, which focuses on middle market lending primarily via the Goldman Sachs Balance Sheet. Justin initially
joined Goldman Sachs in 2006 as an associate and rejoined the firm as a vice president in 2013. He was named managing director in 2019. Prior to rejoining the firm, Mr. Betzen worked at Newstone Capital Partners, focused on second lien, mezzanine
and minority equity investing. Prior to initially joining the firm, he worked at JPMorgan Chase in the Technology Corporate Banking Group, focused on software, services and payments companies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Alex Chi.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Chi serves as the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-chief</FONT> executive officer and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-president.</FONT> Mr.&nbsp;Chi also serves as the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-chief</FONT> executive officer and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-president</FONT> of GS BDC, GS PMMC and GS PMMC II.
Mr.&nbsp;Chi is <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-head</FONT> of Goldman Sachs Asset Management Private Credit in the Americas. Before assuming his current role, Mr.&nbsp;Chi spent 25 years in Goldman Sachs&#146;s Investment Banking Division.
Mr.&nbsp;Chi worked in the Financial and Strategic Investors Group from 2006 to 2019, managing Goldman Sachs&#146;s relationships with private equity and related portfolio company clients. Prior to that, Mr.&nbsp;Chi worked in Leveraged Finance,
where he spent six years structuring and executing leveraged loan and high yield debt financings for corporate and private equity clients across industries. He also spent three years in Asia focused on mergers and acquisitions and corporate finance
transactions. Mr.&nbsp;Chi was named managing director in 2006 and partner in 2012. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Tucker Greene.</B> Mr. Greene is a managing
director in Private Credit within Goldman Sachs Asset Management. He is focused on the firm&#146;s middle market credit investing strategies, including sourcing, structuring and managing senior credit facilities. Mr. Greene joined Goldman Sachs
Asset Management in 2004 in the Specialty Lending Group and was named managing director in 2021. Prior to joining Goldman Sachs Asset Management, Mr. Greene worked at GE Capital. Previously, he was an associate in underwriting and portfolio
management for two years within GE Capital&#146;s Media and Communications Group. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>David Miller.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Miller serves as the
Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-chief</FONT> executive officer and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-president.</FONT> Mr.&nbsp;Miller also serves as the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-chief</FONT> executive officer and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-president</FONT> of GS BDC, GS PMMC and GS PMMC II. Mr.&nbsp;Miller is <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-head</FONT> of Goldman Sachs Asset Management Private Credit in the Americas. He has spent his nearly <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-year</FONT> career as an investor in middle market companies and has originated billions of dollars in commitments across all industries to companies in various stages of the lifecycle. He
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-founded</FONT> in 2004 Goldman Sachs&#146;s middle market origination effort investing primarily firm capital and has led that business since 2013. Prior to joining Goldman Sachs in 2004, Mr.&nbsp;Miller was
senior vice president of originations for GE Capital, where he was responsible for structuring and originating loans in the media and telecommunications sectors. Previously, Mr.&nbsp;Miller was a director at SunTrust Bank, responsible for
originating and managing a portfolio of middle market loans. Mr.&nbsp;Miller was named managing director in 2012 and partner in 2014. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Gabriella Skirnick. </B>Ms.&nbsp;Skirnick serves as the Company&#146;s chief operating officer. Ms.&nbsp;Skirnick will also serves as the
chief operating officer of GS BDC, GS PMMC and GS PMMC II. Ms.&nbsp;Skirnick is global chief operating officer of Goldman Sachs Asset Management Private Credit. Prior to joining the Merchant Banking Division as global chief operating officer of the
Private Credit investing platform in 2017, she spent six years in the Investment Banking Division in the Technology, Media and Telecom Group, where she focused on technology mergers and acquisitions, as well as in the Americas Financing Group.
Ms.&nbsp;Skirnick joined Goldman Sachs as an analyst in the Communications, Media and Entertainment Group within the Investment Banking Division in 2000 and rejoined the firm in 2010. Before <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-joining</FONT> Goldman
Sachs, Ms.&nbsp;Skirnick worked in distressed investing at Aurelius Capital Management and Perella Weinberg Partners. She was named managing director of Goldman Sachs in 2017. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">15 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>David Pessah.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Pessah is the chief financial officer, treasurer and principal
accounting officer of the Company. Mr.&nbsp;Pessah is also the chief financial officer, treasurer principal accounting officer of GS BDC, GS PMMC and GS PMMC II. Mr.&nbsp;Pessah is a vice president in the BDC Fund Controllers team of the Investment
Adviser. Mr.&nbsp;Pessah is responsible for fund accounting and financial reporting oversight as well as the continuous improvement of the control environment for the Company. Prior to joining Goldman Sachs, Mr.&nbsp;Pessah worked in the audit
practice at Ernst&nbsp;&amp; Young LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Julien Yoo.</B> Ms.&nbsp;Yoo is the chief compliance officer of the Company. Ms.&nbsp;Yoo is
Managing Director of GSAM Compliance, Head of the U.S. Regulatory Compliance team with GSAM compliance, and Chief Compliance Officer of GS BDC, GS PMMC and GS PMMC II. Prior to joining Goldman Sachs, Ms.&nbsp;Yoo was a Vice President in the legal
department of Morgan Stanley Investment Management. Prior to joining Morgan Stanley, she was an associate at Shearman&nbsp;&amp; Sterling, LLP and at Swidler Berlin Shereff Friedman, LLP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Greg Watts.</B> Mr. Watts serves as head of underwriting and portfolio management for Goldman Sachs Asset Management Private Credit in the
Americas. He has spent greater than 20 years as a credit investor in middle market companies and has overseen billions of dollars of investments from origination to exit as well as a significant amount of experience in workouts and restructurings.
Mr. Watts is a member of the BDC Investment Committee and the Private Credit Investment Subcommittee, which focuses on middle market lending primarily via the Goldman Sachs Balance Sheet. Mr. Watts joined Goldman Sachs in 2007 and was named managing
director in 2015. Prior to joining the firm, Mr. Watts spent five years with GE Capital&#146;s Technology, Media and Telecom Finance Group as a senior vice president and risk team leader in underwriting and portfolio management. Before working at GE
Capital, Mr. Watts was an associate at Investcorp International after beginning his career as an investment banking analyst in Salomon Smith Barney&#146;s Mergers and Acquisitions Group. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jennifer Yang. </B>Ms. Yang is a managing director in Credit Alternatives within Goldman Sachs Asset Management, with oversight of
Healthcare. She is responsible for leading and managing the healthcare investment strategy and portfolio. Ms. Yang joined Goldman Sachs in 2018 as a vice president and was named managing director in 2021. Prior to joining the firm, Jennifer was an
executive director at Varagon Capital Partners, where she was responsible for structuring, executing and managing credit investments in the healthcare sector. Previously, she was a vice president at Fifth Street Asset Management, focused on
healthcare deal execution. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Certain Relationships and Related Party Transactions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Investment Management Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GSAM serves as our investment adviser. Our Investment Adviser has been registered as an investment adviser with the SEC since 1990 and is a
subsidiary of Group Inc., a bank holding company. GS&nbsp;&amp; Co., a wholly-owned subsidiary of Group Inc., acted as our placement agent in connection with the offering of shares to U.S. persons and Goldman Sachs International, a wholly-owned
subsidiary of Group Inc., acted as our placement agent in connection with the offering of shares to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-U.S.</FONT> persons. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subject to the supervision of the Board of Directors, the Investment Adviser provides <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> advice regarding the Company&#146;s portfolio transactions and is responsible for the Company&#146;s business affairs and other administrative matters. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2022, Management Fees amounted to $0.12&nbsp;million and $0.19&nbsp;million, all of which was
waived by GSAM. For the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2022, Incentive Fees based on capital gains under GAAP were $(0.04)&nbsp;million and $(0.03)&nbsp;million, which was not realized. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the period from October&nbsp;29, 2021 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2021, Management Fees amounted to
$0.01&nbsp;million, all of which was waived by GSAM. For the period from October 29, 2021 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2021, Incentive Fees based on capital gains under GAAP were $0.03&nbsp;million, which was not realized. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>License Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to a license agreement (the &#147;License Agreement&#148;) with an affiliate of Goldman Sachs pursuant to which we have
been granted a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exclusive,</FONT> royalty-free license to use the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. Under this agreement, we shall not have a right to use the Goldman Sachs name if the Investment Adviser or another
affiliate of Goldman Sachs is not our Investment Adviser or if our continued use of such license results in a violation of applicable law, results in a regulatory burden or has adverse regulatory consequences. Other than with respect to this limited
license, we have no legal right to the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Investment</FONT> Opportunities
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In certain circumstances, negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments</FONT> by the Company and other funds managed
by the Investment Adviser may be made only pursuant to an order from the SEC permitting the Company to do so. On January&nbsp;4, 2017, the SEC granted to the Investment Adviser and the BDCs advised by the Investment Adviser exemptive relief on which
we expect to rely to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invest</FONT> with other funds managed by the Investment Adviser in a manner consistent with our investment, objectives, positions, policies, strategies and restrictions as well as regulatory
requirements and other pertinent factors (the &#147;Relief&#148;). Additionally, if our Investment Adviser forms certain other accounts in the future, we may <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invest</FONT> on a concurrent basis with such other
affiliates, subject to compliance with the Relief, applicable regulations and regulatory guidance, as well as applicable allocation procedures. On March&nbsp;15, 2022, the SEC published a notice of an application that is intended to supersede the
Relief and, if granted, would permit limited additional flexibility for the Company to enter into <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investment</FONT> transactions with proprietary accounts of Goldman Sachs (the &#147;Application&#148;). As a
result of the Relief and the Application, if granted, there could be significant overlap in our investment portfolio and the investment portfolios as another client account managed by our Investment Adviser (collectively with the Company, the
&#147;Accounts&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Goldman Sachs Asset Management Private Credit (&#147;GSAM Private Credit&#148;) team is comprised of
investment professionals dedicated to the Company&#146;s investment strategy and other funds that share a similar investment strategy with the Company, who are responsible for identifying investment opportunities, conducting research and due
diligence on prospective investments, negotiating and structuring the Company&#146;s investments and monitoring and servicing the Company&#146;s investments, together with investment professionals who are primarily focused on investment strategies
in syndicated, liquid credit. Under the terms of the Relief and Application, if granted, a &#147;required majority&#148; (as defined in Section&nbsp;57(o) of the Investment Company Act) of the Company&#146;s independent directors must make certain
conclusions in connection with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investment</FONT> transaction, including that (1)&nbsp;the terms of the proposed transaction are reasonable and fair to the Company and the Company&#146;s stockholders and do not
involve overreaching in respect of the Company or its stockholders on the part of any person concerned, and (2)&nbsp;the transaction is consistent with the interests of the Company&#146;s stockholders and is consistent with the then-current
investment objectives and strategies of the Company </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Transfer Agent Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has entered into a transfer agency agreement (the &#147;Transfer Agency Agreement&#148;), with Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, an
affiliate of GSAM, pursuant to which Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, serves as the Company&#146;s transfer agent (&#147;Transfer Agent&#148;), registrar and disbursing agent. The Company pays the Transfer Agent fees at an annual rate of 0.15% of
the average NAV of the Company at the end of the then-current quarter and the prior calendar quarter (and, in the case of the Company&#146;s first quarter, the Company&#146;s NAV as of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">such&nbsp;quarter-end).</FONT>
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2022, the Company incurred expenses for services provided by the Transfer Agent of
$0.02&nbsp;million and $0.04&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the period from October 29, 2021 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2021,
the Company incurred expenses for services provided by the Transfer Agent of $0.01&nbsp;million. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Placement Agent Agreements </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has entered into an agreement with each of Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC and Goldman Sachs International (each, a
&#147;Placement Agent&#148; and together with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">various&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agents,</FONT> the &#147;Placement Agents&#148;) pursuant to which the Placement Agents will assist the Company in conducting private
placement offerings. The Placement Agents have entered into or will enter <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">into&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agreements</FONT> (together with the agreements with Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC and Goldman Sachs
International, the &#147;Placement Agent Agreements&#148;) with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">various&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agents</FONT> to assist in conducting the private placement offering. The Placement Agents are not expected to be
compensated by the Company for their services, but may charge investors a placement fee with respect to their investment in the Company. The Placement Agents may also be compensated by the Investment Adviser, in its discretion, for certain services
including promotional and marketing support, shareholder servicing, operational and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">recordkeeping,&nbsp;sub-accounting,&nbsp;networking</FONT> or administrative services. These payments are made out of the Investment
Adviser&#146;s own resources and/or assets, including from the revenues or profits derived from the advisory fees the Investment Adviser receives from the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Related Party Transaction Review Policy </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee will conduct quarterly review any potential related party transactions brought to its attention and, during these reviews,
it also considers any conflicts of interest brought to its attention pursuant to the Company&#146;s Code of Ethics. Each of our directors and executive officers will complete a questionnaire on an annual basis designed to elicit information about
any potential related party transactions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Proxy Voting by the Investment Adviser </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our Investment Adviser has implemented processes designed to prevent conflicts of interest from influencing proxy voting decisions that it
makes on behalf of advisory clients, including us, and to help ensure that such decisions are made in accordance with its fiduciary obligations to its clients. Notwithstanding such proxy voting processes, proxy voting decisions made by our
Investment Adviser with respect to securities held by us may benefit the interests of Goldman Sachs and Accounts other than us. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">18 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROPOSAL 2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>RATIFICATION OF SELECTION OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At a meeting of the Board held on August <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-3,</FONT> 2022, the Audit Committee selected and recommended, and
the Board, including a majority of the Independent Directors, approved, the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to act as the independent registered public accounting firm for the Company for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2022. This
selection is presented for ratification by the Stockholders. If the Stockholders fail to ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the independent registered public accounting firm for the year ending December&nbsp;31, 2022, the
Audit Committee and the Board will reconsider the continued retention of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Representatives of
PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP are expected to be present at the Meeting and will be available to respond to appropriate questions from Stockholders if necessary. Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP will be given the opportunity to make
statements at the Meeting, if they so desire. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Fees </I></B></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the audit fees category are those associated with the annual audits of financial statements and services that are normally
provided in connection with statutory and regulatory filings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit-Related Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No audit-related fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the year ended December 31, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Audit-related fees are for any services rendered to the Company that are reasonably related to the performance of the audits or reviews of the
Company&#146;s financial statements (but not reported as audit fees above). These services include attestation services that are not required by statute or regulation and consultations concerning financial accounting and reporting standards. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit-related fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common
control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2021 were $1,337,432. These amounts represent fees
PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP billed to GSAM for services related to the SSAE 18 report. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">19 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Tax Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for services rendered to the Company for tax compliance, tax advice and tax planning for the
year ended December 31, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the tax fees category comprise all services performed by professional staff in the
independent registered public accountant&#146;s tax division except those services related to the audits. This category comprises fees for tax compliance services provided in connection with the preparation and review of the Company&#146;s tax
returns. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No tax fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public accountant to GSAM, and any entity controlling,
controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the period from October&nbsp;29, 2021 (commencement of
operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>All Other Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for products and services provided to the Company, other than the services reported in
&#147;Audit Fees,&#148; &#147;Audit Related Fees,&#148; and &#147;Tax Fees&#148; above, for the year ended December 31, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other than
services reported under &#147;Audit-Related Fees,&#148; no other fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public accountant to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides
ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the period from October&nbsp;29, 2021 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Aggregate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> fees were billed to the GSAM and service affiliates by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services for the period from October&nbsp;29, 2021 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2021. This includes any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services required to be <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services that did not require <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> since they did not directly relate to the Company&#146;s
operations or financial reporting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> of Audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT>
Services Provided to the Company </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;Non-Audit&nbsp;Services&nbsp;Pre-Approval&nbsp;Policy</FONT></FONT> (the &#147;Policy&#148;) adopted by the Audit Committee sets forth the procedures and the conditions
pursuant to which services performed by an independent auditor for the Company may <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved.&nbsp;Services</FONT> may <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;specifically</FONT> by the
Audit Committee as a whole or, in certain circumstances, by the Audit Committee Chairman or the person designated as the audit committee financial expert. In addition, subject to specified cost limitations, certain services may <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;under</FONT> the provisions of the Policy. The Policy provides that the Audit Committee will consider whether the services provided by an independent auditor are consistent with the SEC&#146;s
rules on auditor independence. The Policy provides for periodic review <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;by</FONT> the Audit Committee of the services that may be provided by the independent auditor. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>De Minimis Waiver</I>. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;requirements</FONT> of the Policy may be waived with
respect to the provision <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> that are permissible for an independent auditor to perform, provided (1)&nbsp;the aggregate amount of all such services provided constitutes no more
than five percent of the total amount of revenues subject <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">to&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;that</FONT> was paid to the independent auditors during the fiscal year in which the services are provided; (2)&nbsp;such services
were not recognized by the Company at the time of the engagement to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services;</FONT> and (3)&nbsp;such services are promptly brought to the attention of the Audit Committee and
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">20 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
approved prior to the completion of the audit by the Audit Committee or by one or more members of the Audit Committee to whom authority to grant such approvals has been delegated by the Audit
Committee, pursuant to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;provisions</FONT> of the Policy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT></I><I></I><I>&nbsp;of</I><I></I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&nbsp;Non-Audit</FONT></I><I></I><I>&nbsp;Services Provided to GSAM.</I>&nbsp;The Policy provides that, in addition to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">requiring&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;of</FONT> audit <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> provided to the Company, the Audit Committee <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">will&nbsp;pre-approve&nbsp;those&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT></FONT> provided to the Company&#146;s investment adviser (and entities controlling, controlled by or under common control with the investment adviser
that provide ongoing services to the Company) where the engagement relates directly to the operations or financial reporting of the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has considered these fees and the nature of the services rendered, and has concluded that they are compatible with
maintaining the independence of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. The Audit Committee did not approve any of the audit-related, tax, or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;fees</FONT> described above pursuant to the &#147;<I>de
minimis</I>&nbsp;exceptions&#148; set forth in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(i)(C)&nbsp;and</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(ii)&nbsp;of</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Regulation&nbsp;S-X.</FONT> PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP did not provide any audit-related services, tax services or other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services to GSAM or any entity controlling,
controlled by or under common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that the Audit Committee was required to approve pursuant to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(ii)&nbsp;of</FONT> <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Regulation&nbsp;S-X.&nbsp;The</FONT> Audit Committee considered whether the provision <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> rendered to GSAM and any entity controlling, controlled by, or
under common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that were <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">not&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;by</FONT> the Audit Committee because the engagement did not relate directly to the operations and
financial reporting of the Company is compatible with maintaining PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP&#146;s independence. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THE BOARD, INCLUDING
EACH OF THE INDEPENDENT DIRECTORS, UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMENDS THAT YOU VOTE&nbsp;&#147;FOR&#148;&nbsp;THE RATIFICATION OF PRICEWATERHOUSECOOPERS LLP AS INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM TO THE COMPANY FOR THE FISCAL YEAR ENDING
DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2022. </B></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">21 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I>Audit Committee Report&nbsp;<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(1)</SUP>
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following is the report of the Audit Committee of Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp. II (the &#147;Company&#148;) with
respect to the Company&#146;s audited financial statements as of December&nbsp;31, 2021 (the &#147;Audited Financial Statements&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has: (a)&nbsp;reviewed and discussed the Audited Financial Statements with the management of the Company;
(b)&nbsp;discussed with the independent auditor the matters required to be discussed by the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (&#147;PCAOB&#148;) Standard No.&nbsp;1301, as modified or supplemented; and (c)&nbsp;received the written
disclosures and the letter from the independent auditor required by applicable requirements of the PCAOB Ethics and Independence Rule 3526 regarding the independent auditor&#146;s communications with the Audit Committee concerning independence, and
has discussed with the independent auditor the auditor&#146;s independence. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The members of the Audit Committee are not, and do not
represent themselves to be, professionally engaged in the practice of auditing or accounting and are not employed by the Company for accounting, financial management or internal control purposes. Moreover, the Audit Committee relies on and makes no
independent verification of the facts presented to it or representations made by management or the Company&#146;s independent auditor. Accordingly, the Audit Committee&#146;s oversight does not provide an independent basis to determine that
management has maintained appropriate accounting and/or financial reporting principles and policies, or internal controls and procedures designed to assure compliance with accounting standards and applicable laws and regulations. Furthermore, the
Audit Committee&#146;s considerations and discussions referred to above do not provide assurance that the audit of the Company&#146;s financial statements has been carried out in accordance with the standards of the PCAOB or that the financial
statements are presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Based on its consideration of the Audited Financial
Statements and the discussions referred to above with management and the Company&#146;s independent auditor, and subject to the limitations on the responsibilities and role of the Audit Committee set forth in the charter and those discussed above,
the Audit Committee recommended to the Board of Directors that the Audited Financial Statements be accepted by the Board of Directors and included in the Company&#146;s Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the last
fiscal year for filing with the SEC. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">August&nbsp;3, 2022 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>The Audit Committee </B></P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OTHER BUSINESS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The management of the Company does not know of any other matters to be brought before the Meeting. If such matters are properly brought before
the Meeting, proxies that do not contain specific instructions to the contrary will be voted in accordance with the judgment of Caroline Kraus and Lindsey Edwards, who are the persons named as proxies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>VOTE REQUIRED FOR THE ELECTION OF DIRECTORS AND APPROVAL OF OTHER MATTERS AT THE MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A quorum for the transaction of business at the Meeting is established by the presence, virtually or by proxy, of holders representing a
majority of the votes entitled to be cast at the Meeting. Stockholders of record at the close of business on the Record Date are entitled to receive notice of, and to vote at, the Meeting and at any postponements or adjournments thereof.&nbsp;There
were 4,118,321 shares of the Company&#146;s common stock outstanding on the Record Date. Each share of common stock is entitled to one vote. Cumulative voting is not permitted. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Election of Directors </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The election of
each nominee requires a majority of the votes cast by all Stockholders present, virtually or by proxy, at the Meeting, provided that if, as of the tenth (10th)&nbsp;day preceding the date the Company first mails the notice of such meeting to the
Stockholders, the number of nominees for the directorships (or, if applicable, the directorships of a particular class of directors) exceeds the number of such directors to be elected, such directors shall be elected by the vote of a plurality of
the votes cast. Under the Company&#146;s bylaws, a majority of votes cast means that the number of votes cast &#147;for&#148; a director&#146;s election exceeds the number of votes cast &#147;against&#148; that director&#146;s election (with
&#147;abstentions&#148; and &#147;broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes&#148;</FONT> not counted as a vote cast either &#147;for&#148; or &#147;against&#148; that director&#146;s election). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ratification of Auditor </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Approval of
Proposal 2, the ratification of the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the Company&#146;s independent registered public accounting firm, requires a majority of the votes cast by all Stockholders present, virtually or by proxy, at
the Meeting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Votes</FONT> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;non-votes&#148;</FONT> are shares held in an account with an Authorized Institution for which the
broker indicates that instructions have not been received from the beneficial owners or other persons entitled to vote, and the broker does not have discretionary voting authority with respect to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-routine</FONT>
proposal. As broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes</FONT> are entitled to vote on Proposal 2, broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes</FONT> will be counted as shares present for purposes of determining whether a quorum is
present. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Proposal 1 is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-routine</FONT> matter. As a result, if you hold shares in &#147;street
name&#148; through a broker, bank or other nominee, your broker, bank or nominee will<B></B><B>&nbsp;not</B>&nbsp;be permitted to exercise voting discretion with respect to Proposal 1, the election of six directors. Therefore, if you do not vote and
you do not give your broker or other nominee specific instructions on how to vote for you, then your shares will have no effect on Proposal 1. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Proposal 2, the ratification of the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the Company&#146;s independent registered public
accounting firm, is a routine matter. As a result, if you beneficially own your shares and you do not provide your broker or nominee with voting instructions, then your broker, bank or nominee will be able to vote your shares for you on Proposal 2.
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">23 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Abstentions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Abstentions will be counted as shares present for purposes of determining whether a quorum is present, but will not be voted for or against the
Proposal for which the proxy card has been marked &#147;Abstain&#148;. Accordingly, abstentions will have no effect on either Proposal. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Adjournment
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If less than a quorum is present at the Meeting or if an insufficient number of votes is present for the approval of the Proposals,
the chairman of the Meeting shall have the power to adjourn the Meeting from time to time without notice other than announcement at the Meeting. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A vote may be taken on either Proposal prior to any such adjournment if there are sufficient votes for approval of such Proposal. </P>

individual director, by addressing such communication to the Board, the Independent Directors, the Chairperson or to the individual director, c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282. </P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">655-4702.</FONT> Please direct your written request to Caroline L. Kraus, Secretary, at the Company, c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282. Copies of such reports are
also posted and are available without charge on the SEC&#146;s website at www.sec.gov. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>CORPORATE GOVERNANCE </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Code of Ethics </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have adopted a code of
ethics pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> under the Investment Company Act and have also approved the Investment Adviser&#146;s code of ethics in accordance with Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> and Rule
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">204A-1</FONT> under the Advisers Act. These codes of ethics establish, among other things, procedures for personal investments and restrict certain personal securities transactions, including transactions in
securities that are held by us. Personnel subject to each code may invest in securities for their personal investment accounts, so long as such investments are made in accordance with the code&#146;s requirements. A copy of our Code of Ethics is
filed as an exhibit to the Company&#146;s annual report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Code of Business Conduct and Ethics
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have adopted a Code of Business Conduct and Ethics which applies to, among others, our Chief Executive Officer and Chief Financial
Officer. We intend to disclose any material amendment to or waivers of required provisions of the Code of Business Conduct and Ethics on a current report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K.</FONT> Our Code of Business Conduct and Ethics is
filed as an exhibit to the Company&#146;s annual report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT><I>.</I> </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Appendix A </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp. II </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Audit Committee Charter </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Organization and Purpose </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board of
Directors (the &#147;Board&#148;) of Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp. II<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> (the &#147;Company&#148;), has established an Audit Committee (the &#147;Committee&#148;), comprised of each of
the Company&#146;s Independent Directors. Independent Directors are those Directors who meet the independence standards set forth in the Company&#146;s Governance and Nominating Committee Charter. The Committee has been established by and among the
Directors for the purpose of overseeing the accounting and financial reporting processes of the Company, the work of the Company&#146;s independent auditors, and the work of the internal auditors relating to the Company. The Board, with the
assistance of the Committee, shall determine whether any member of the Committee is an &#147;audit committee financial expert&#148; (&#147;ACFE&#148;) as defined by the applicable regulations of the Securities and Exchange Commission (the
&#147;SEC&#148;). The Committee will select one of its members to be its chair. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Committee will set its agenda and the places and
times of its meetings. The greater of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-third</FONT> or two members of the Committee shall constitute a quorum. Except as otherwise required by applicable law, the Committee shall act by a vote of a majority of the
Committee members at a Committee meeting, including a meeting held by conference telephone, teleconference or other electronic media or communication equipment, or by written consent of all of the Committee members without a meeting. Any written
consent or waiver may be provided and delivered to the Committee chair by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-mail,</FONT> facsimile or other similar electronic mechanism. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Statement of Policy </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Committee shall
oversee the audit process and provide assistance to the Board in fulfilling its responsibilities in overseeing financial reporting. The Committee will also assist the Board with the oversight of the Company&#146;s compliance with regulatory
requirements that relate to the Company accounting and financial reporting, internal control over financial reporting and independent audits. In so doing, the Committee will endeavor to facilitate free and open means of communication among the
Company&#146;s Directors, independent registered public accounting firm (the &#147;independent auditor&#148;), and management. A primary objective of the Committee is to help set the &#147;tone at the top&#148; for quality financial reporting and a
sound system of internal controls over financial reporting. The Committee will regularly report its activities, observations, and recommendations to the Board. The Committee&#146;s activities and effectiveness will be assessed periodically and
reviewed with the Board. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Summary of Responsibilities </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The function of the Committee is oversight. Management of the Company (&#147;Management&#148;) is responsible for the preparation,
presentation, and integrity of the Company&#146;s financial statements. Management draws upon different parts of the Goldman Sachs corporate structure in fulfilling this role &#151; the Controllers department (within the Finance Division) and the
Operations Division (working in conjunction with Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (&#147;GSAM&#148;) Global Fund Services) are responsible for applying appropriate accounting and financial reporting principles and maintaining policies and
internal controls and procedures designed to assure compliance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) and applicable laws and regulations. In fulfilling its role under this Audit Committee Charter (the &#147;Charter&#148;), Management
also delegates certain functions to the Company&#146;s accounting agents, but remains responsible for those functions. The independent </P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">For periods before its conversion from a limited liability company to a corporation, Goldman Sachs Middle
Market Lending LLC II. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">26 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
auditor for the Company is responsible for planning and executing audits consistent with applicable professional standards and in accordance with the terms of the engagement letter(s). The
independent auditor will report directly to the Committee. The Committee shall provide for appropriate funding for the payment of compensation to the independent auditor, any other counsel or advisors engaged by the Committee at its discretion, and
the ordinary administrative expenses of the Committee as necessary or appropriate in carrying out its duties. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Committee performs its
functions under this Charter on the basis of information provided or representations made to it by the Company&#146;s independent auditor, Management, and/or other service providers, and/or by legal counsel and/or other experts or consultants.
Nothing in this Charter is intended to impose, or should be interpreted as imposing, on any member of the Committee (including any member designated as an ACFE) any additional duties or responsibilities over and above those placed on the member in
his or her capacity as a Board member of the Company under applicable federal and state law. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subject to regulatory mandates, the policies
and procedures of the Committee should remain flexible in order to react to changing conditions and to assist the Committee in providing assurance to the Board and shareholders that the Company&#146;s accounting and reporting practices are in
accordance with applicable requirements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are the duties and responsibilities of the Committee: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><U>Primarily Related to the Independent Auditor </U></I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Evaluate and select (subject to ratification by the Board) the Company&#146;s independent auditor.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Participate in the selection process and approve the new lead audit partner(s) as a result of mandatory audit
partner rotation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Be responsible for the appointment, compensation, retention and oversight of the work of the independent
auditor engaged (including resolution of disagreements between Management and the auditor regarding financial reporting) for the purpose of rendering or issuing an audit report or performing other audit or attest services for the Company. The
independent auditor must report directly to the Committee. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">At least annually, obtain and review a report by the independent auditor describing the auditor&#146;s internal
quality-control procedures, as well as any material issues raised by the most recent internal quality-control review or peer review of the auditor, or by any inquiry or investigation by governmental or professional authorities, including the Public
Company Accounting Oversight Board (&#147;PCAOB&#148;), within the preceding five years, with respect to one or more independent audits carried out by the auditor, and any steps taken to deal with any such issues. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Review and approve the compensation of (a)&nbsp;the independent auditor employed by the Company for the purpose
of rendering or issuing an audit report and any other services that they may perform and (b)&nbsp;any advisers employed by the Committee as described herein. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Evaluate the performance of the auditor in light of the report identified in Item 3 above and its work
throughout the year, as well as the auditor&#146;s lead partner, evaluate the independence and qualifications of the auditor, including its processes to remain independent, and request an annual representation from the independent auditor regarding
its independence under applicable professional and regulatory standards. As part of its evaluation of the independence of the auditor, the Committee may inquire into and consider such items as: (1)&nbsp;the audit and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services performed by the auditor and related fees; (2)&nbsp;the hiring of partners or employees or former partners or employees of the auditor by the Company and its affiliates; (3)&nbsp;whether any
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services provided by the auditor to the Company&#146;s investment adviser or any adviser affiliate that provides ongoing services to the Company are compatible with maintaining the auditor&#146;s
independence; (4)&nbsp;the rotation of the auditor&#146;s partners who participate in providing auditing services to the Company; and (5)&nbsp;other relationships, if any, between the Company and the auditor that may bear on the independence or
objectivity of the auditor. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">27 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Set policies governing the hiring by entities within the Company&#146;s Investment Company Complex<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> of any current or former employee of the Company&#146;s independent auditor, and to assess compliance with these policies. These policies provide, among other things, that no former employee of the
independent auditor who was a member of the Company&#146;s audit engagement team may undertake any financial reporting role at the Company within one year of the date of the commencement of procedures for a review or audit. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Meet with the independent auditor and financial and accounting personnel of the Company to review the scope of
the proposed audits for the current year, the audit procedures to be utilized, and the key risk considerations, and at the conclusion thereof, review the results of such audit, including the independent auditor&#146;s opinions on the Company&#146;s
financial statements and any management letters, comments, or recommendations of the independent auditor and consider Management&#146;s response to such. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Meet at least four times annually with Management and the independent auditor, or more frequently if
circumstances dictate, and meet at least annually with the independent auditor (or more frequently if circumstances dictate) alone and outside the presence of Management personnel in executive session, to discuss any problems or difficulties the
independent auditor encountered in the course of the audit work, including any restrictions on the scope of the independent auditor&#146;s activities or access to requested information and any significant disagreements with Management, whether or
not satisfactorily resolved, about matters that individually or in the aggregate could be significant to the Company&#146;s financial statements, the effectiveness of internal controls, including internal controls over financial reporting, and the
audit report(s) of the independent auditor, and Management&#146;s response. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Review and discuss with Management and the Company&#146;s independent auditor the Company&#146;s audited annual
financial statements, including the Company&#146;s disclosure of management&#146;s discussion of Company performance and the effect of regulatory and accounting initiatives, as well as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">off-balance</FONT> sheet
structures, on the financial statements of the Company. Review and discuss with Management the Company&#146;s unaudited quarterly financial statements, including the Company&#146;s disclosure of management&#146;s discussion of Company performance.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">11.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Oversee the preparation of the Audit Committee report required to be included in the Company&#146;s proxy
statement for its annual meeting of shareholders (if such meeting is required by law). The report shall indicate whether the Committee has (i)&nbsp;reviewed and discussed the financial statements with management; (ii)&nbsp;discussed with the
independent auditor the matters required to be discussed by the PCAOB Standard No.&nbsp;16, as modified or supplemented; and (iii)&nbsp;received written disclosures and the letter from the independent auditor required by applicable requirements of
the PCAOB Ethics and Independence Rule 3526 regarding the independent auditor&#146;s communications with the Committee concerning independence, and has discussed with the independent auditor the auditor&#146;s independence. The Committee&#146;s
report should also indicate whether the Committee, based on its review and its discussions with management and the independent auditor, recommends to the Board that the financial statements be included in the Company&#146;s annual report for the
last fiscal year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">&#147;Investment company complex&#148; includes: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">the Company and its investment adviser or sponsor; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">any entity controlling, controlled by or under common control with the investment adviser or sponsor, if the
entity: (i) is an investment adviser or sponsor; or (ii) is engaged in the business of providing administrative, custodian, underwriting or transfer agent services to any investment company, investment adviser or sponsor; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">any investment company, hedge fund or unregistered fund that has an investment adviser included in the definition
set forth in either of the two bullet points above. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">An investment adviser, for these purposes, does not include a sub-adviser whose role
is primarily portfolio management and that is subcontracted with or overseen by another investment adviser. Sponsor refers to the sponsor of a unit investment trust. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">28 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">12.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Review and discuss with Management and the Company&#146;s independent auditor any major issues regarding
accounting principles and financial statement presentations, including any significant changes in the Company&#146;s selection or application of accounting principles, and major issues as to the adequacy of the Company&#146;s internal controls over
financial reporting and any special audit steps adopted in light of material control deficiencies. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Consider and, if appropriate, recommend to the Board the publication of the Company&#146;s annual audited
financial statements in the Company&#146;s annual report in advance of the printing and publication of the annual report, based on its review and discussions of such annual report with the independent auditor and Management. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

Committee or the Board. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

relating to the Company&#146;s financial statements, including any adjustments to such statements recommended by the auditor, or other results of said audit(s), including matters required to be discussed under the PCAOB Standard No.&nbsp;16.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Review with financial and accounting personnel and the independent auditor the quality, not just the
acceptability, of accounting principles and financial disclosure practices used or proposed to be used by the Company. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Review with the independent auditor, and financial and accounting personnel the adequacy and effectiveness of
the accounting and financial controls of the Company, and consider any recommendations for the improvement of the Company&#146;s internal control procedures or particular areas where new or more detailed controls or procedures are desirable.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

of internal controls to identify any payments, transactions or procedures that might be deemed fraudulent, illegal or otherwise improper. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

and compliance procedures used for the Company. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><U>Primarily Related to Management and/or Internal Audit </U></I></B></P>

performed by Internal Audit as it relates to the Company&#146;s control environment. After the conclusion of these audits, discuss the significant results of the audits and Management&#146;s responses thereto. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

officer and principal financial officer, based on their periodic evaluations, regarding: (a)&nbsp;any significant deficiencies and material weaknesses in the design or operation of internal control over financial reporting which are reasonably
likely to adversely affect the Company&#146;s ability to record, process, summarize, and report financial information; and (b)&nbsp;any fraud, whether or not material, that involves Management or other employees who have a significant role in the

Company&#146;s service providers. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><U>Other </U></I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

director or Board member of the Company or its investment adviser or distributor/placement agent, or any person acting under their direction, may have violated applicable regulatory provisions prohibiting: (a) materially false or misleading
statements or omissions in connection with any audit of the Company&#146;s financial statements or the preparation of any document or report required to be filed with a regulatory body; or (b)&nbsp;actions to fraudulently influence, coerce,
manipulate or mislead the Company&#146;s independent auditor in connection with their opining on the Company&#146;s financial statements. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

(a)&nbsp;accounting, internal controls, or auditing matters relating to the Company; (b)&nbsp;other legal, compliance, and ethical issues relating to the Company; and (c)&nbsp;instances of suspected financial statement or other fraud relating to the
Company. The Committee shall review whether the procedures provide for the confidential, anonymous submission of complaints by officers and Directors of the Company, employees of The Goldman Sachs Group, Inc. and its affiliates and, as applicable,
other persons covered by the procedures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

control such exposures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
